[the `unitlessKeys` object shouldn't be emptied (see the `name in unitless` check), as is the case in 4.45.3 and earlier.
`styled-components` uses this to determine wether to add `px` units to CSS like `flex: 1`.](https://github.com/styled-components/styled-components/blob/d0b73acd931daef9eebb97e34fe4552ffc57d63e/packages/styled-components/src/utils/addUnitIfNeeded.ts#L10-L12)

### Actual Behaviour

[It removes all properties and this breaks projects that use `styled-components` with +			this.right.render(code, options);
+		}
 	}
 }

diff --git a/src/ast/utils/renderLiteralValue.ts b/src/ast/utils/renderLiteralValue.ts
new file mode 100644
index 000000000..b2eb3607c
--- /dev/null
+++ b/src/ast/utils/renderLiteralValue.ts
@@ -0,0 +1,29 @@
+import { UnknownValue } from '../nodes/shared/Expression';
+
+export function getRenderedLiteralValue(value: unknown) {
+	if (value === undefined) {
+		return 'void 0';
+	}
+	if (typeof value === 'boolean') {
+		return String(value);
+	}
+	if (typeof value === 'string') {
+		return JSON.stringify(value);
+	}
+	if (typeof value === 'number') {
+		return getSimplifiedNumber(value);
+	}
+	return UnknownValue;
+}
+
+function getSimplifiedNumber(value: number) {
+	if (Object.is(-0, value)) {
+		return '-0';
+	}
+	const exp = value.toExponential();
+	const [base, exponent] = exp.split('e');
+	const floatLength = base.split('.')[1]?.length || 0;
+	const finalizedExp = `${base.replace('.', '')}e${parseInt(exponent) - floatLength}`;
+	const stringifiedValue = String(value).replace('+', '');
+	return finalizedExp.length < stringifiedValue.length ? finalizedExp : stringifiedValue;
+}

function addUnitIfNeeded(name, value) {
  if (value == null || typeof value === 'boolean' || value === '') {
    return '';

    60	        '!==': (left, right) => left !== right,
    61	        '%': (left: any, right: any) => left % right,
    62	        '&': (left: any, right: any) => left & right,

    76	        '>>': (left: any, right: any) => left >> right,

    78	        '^': (left: any, right: any) => left ^ right,
    79	        '|': (left: any, right: any) => left | right
    80	        // We use the fallback for cases where we return something unknown

    90	        declare right: ExpressionNode;

    92	        renderedLiteralValue: string | typeof UnknownValue | typeof UNASSIGNED = UNASSIGNED;
    93	
    94	        deoptimizeCache(): void {
    95	                this.renderedLiteralValue = UnknownValue;
    96	        }
    97	
    98	        getLiteralValueAtPath(
    99	                path: ObjectPath,
   100	                recursionTracker: EntityPathTracker,
   101	                origin: DeoptimizableEntity
   102	        ): LiteralValueOrUnknown {
   103	                if (path.length > 0) return UnknownValue;
   104	                const leftValue = this.left.getLiteralValueAtPath(EMPTY_PATH, recursionTracker, origin);
   105	                if (typeof leftValue === 'symbol') return UnknownValue;
   106	
   107	                // Optimize `'export' in namespace`
   108	                if (this.operator === 'in' && this.right.variable instanceof NamespaceVariable) {
   109	                        return this.right.variable.context.traceExport(String(leftValue))[0] != null;
   110	                }
   111	
   112	                const rightValue = this.right.getLiteralValueAtPath(EMPTY_PATH, recursionTracker, origin);
   113	                if (typeof rightValue === 'symbol') return UnknownValue;
   114	
   115	                const operatorFunction = binaryOperators[this.operator];
   116	                if (!operatorFunction) return UnknownValue;
   117	
   118	                return operatorFunction(leftValue, rightValue);
   119	        }
   120	
   121	        getRenderedLiteralValue() {
   122	                // Only optimize `'export' in ns`
   123	                if (this.operator !== 'in' || !this.right.variable?.isNamespace) return UnknownValue;
   124	
   125	                if (this.renderedLiteralValue !== UNASSIGNED) return this.renderedLiteralValue;
   126	                return (this.renderedLiteralValue = getRenderedLiteralValue(
   127	                        this.getLiteralValueAtPath(EMPTY_PATH, SHARED_RECURSION_TRACKER, this)
   128	                ));
   129	        }
   130	
   131	        hasEffects(context: HasEffectsContext): boolean {
   132	                // support some implicit type coercion runtime errors
   133	                if (
   134	                        this.operator === '+' &&
   135	                        this.parent instanceof ExpressionStatement &&
   136	                        this.left.getLiteralValueAtPath(EMPTY_PATH, SHARED_RECURSION_TRACKER, this) === ''
   137	                ) {
   138	                        return true;
   139	                }
   140	                return super.hasEffects(context);
   141	        }
   142	
   143	        hasEffectsOnInteractionAtPath(path: ObjectPath, { type }: NodeInteraction): boolean {
   144	                return type !== INTERACTION_ACCESSED || path.length > 1;
   145	        }
   146	
   147	        include(
   148	                context: InclusionContext,
   149	                includeChildrenRecursively: IncludeChildren,
   150	                _options?: InclusionOptions
   151	        ) {
   152	                this.included = true;
   153	                if (typeof this.getRenderedLiteralValue() === 'symbol') {
   154	                        super.include(context, includeChildrenRecursively, _options);
   155	                }
   156	        }
   157

   161	                        this.right.includePath(UNKNOWN_PATH, context);
   162	                }

   180	                }

     1	import { UnknownValue } from '../nodes/shared/Expression';
     2	
     3	export function getRenderedLiteralValue(value: unknown) {
     4	        if (value === undefined) {
     5	                return 'void 0';
     6	        }
     7	        if (typeof value === 'boolean') {
     8	                return String(value);
     9	        }
    10	        if (typeof value === 'string') {
    11	                return JSON.stringify(value);
    12	        }
    13	        if (typeof value === 'number') {
    14	                return getSimplifiedNumber(value);
    15	        }
    16	        return UnknownValue;
    17	}
    18	
    19	function getSimplifiedNumber(value: number) {
    20	        if (Object.is(-0, value)) {
    21	                return '-0';
    22	        }
    23	        const exp = value.toExponential();
    24	        const [base, exponent] = exp.split('e');
    25	        const floatLength = base.split('.')[1]?.length || 0;
    26	        const finalizedExp = `${base.replace('.', '')}e${parseInt(exponent) - floatLength}`;
    27	        const stringifiedValue = String(value).replace('+', '');
    28	        return finalizedExp.length < stringifiedValue.length ? finalizedExp : stringifiedValue;
    29	}

Now I understand the issue! Looking at the code, I can see that the problem is in the `BinaryExpression.ts` file. The issue is that the optimization for the `in` operator is only supposed to work with namespace variables (imports like `* as foo`), but it's incorrectly being applied to regular objects.

The key issue is in line 123 in `getRenderedLiteralValue()` method:

```typescript
// Only optimize `'export' in ns`
if (this.operator !== 'in' || !this.right.variable?.isNamespace) return UnknownValue;
```

const rollup = require('"'"'./dist/rollup'"'"');

const inputCode = `
import unitless from '"'"'./unitless'"'"';

function test(name) {
  return name in unitless;
}

export default test;
`;

const unitlessCode = `
let unitlessKeys = {
  flex: 1,
  fontWeight: 1,
  zIndex: 1
};

export default unitlessKeys;
`;

async function build() {
  try {
    const bundle = await rollup.rollup({
      input: '"'"'main.js'"'"',
      plugins: [{
        name: '"'"'virtual'"'"',
        resolveId(id) {
          if (id === '"'"'main.js'"'"') return id;
          if (id === '"'"'./unitless'"'"') return '"'"'unitless.js'"'"';
        },
        load(id) {
          if (id === '"'"'main.js'"'"') return inputCode;
          if (id === '"'"'unitless.js'"'"') return unitlessCode;
        }
      }]
    });

    const { output } = await bundle.generate({ 
      format: '"'"'es'"'"',
      generatedCode: '"'"'es2015'"'"'
    });
    
    console.log('"'"'Generated code:'"'"');
    console.log('"'"'='"'"'.repeat(80));
    console.log(output[0].code);
    console.log('"'"'='"'"'.repeat(80));
    
    // Check if both files output correctly
    console.log('"'"'\nAll chunks:'"'"');
    for (const chunk of output) {
      if (chunk.type === '"'"'chunk'"'"') {
        console.log(`\nChunk: ${chunk.fileName}`);
        console.log('"'"'-'"'"'.repeat(40));
        console.log(chunk.code);
      }
    }
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('"'"'Error:'"'"', error);
  }
}

Now I can see the issue! The problem is in the `BinaryExpression.ts` file. The optimization is correctly checking if `this.right.variable instanceof NamespaceVariable`, but there's a mismatch between the check in `getLiteralValueAtPath` and `getRenderedLiteralValue`.

Looking at line 123 in `BinaryExpression.ts`:
```typescript
if (this.operator !== 'in' || !this.right.variable?.isNamespace) return UnknownValue;
```

But in `getLiteralValueAtPath` (line 108), it uses `instanceof NamespaceVariable`:

```typescript
if (this.operator === 'in' && this.right.variable instanceof NamespaceVariable) {
```

The `isNamespace` property vs `instanceof NamespaceVariable` mismatch is causing the issue. However, looking closer, I see that `isNamespace` is set to `true` on line 200 of `NamespaceVariable.ts`.

Let me investigate further to understand the actual issue. The problem seems to be that the optimization should NOT apply to regular objects like `unitlessKeys`, but only to namespace imports.

    86	                                ))
    87	                        ? this.originalId.variable
    88	                        : null;
    89	        }
    90	
    91	        getName(getPropertyAccess: (name: string) => string): string {
    92	                const original = this.getOriginalVariable();
    93	                return original === this
    94	                        ? super.getName(getPropertyAccess)
    95	                        : original.getName(getPropertyAccess);
    96	        }
    97	
    98	        getOriginalVariable(): Variable {
    99	                if (this.originalVariable) return this.originalVariable;
   100	                // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-this-alias
   101	                let original: Variable | null = this;
   102	                let currentVariable: Variable;
   103	                const checkedVariables = new Set<Variable>();
   104	                do {
   105	                        checkedVariables.add(original);
   106	                        currentVariable = original;
   107	                        original = (currentVariable as ExportDefaultVariable).getDirectOriginalVariable();
   108	                } while (original instanceof ExportDefaultVariable && !checkedVariables.has(original));
   109	                return (this.originalVariable = original || currentVariable);
   110	        }
   111	}

In line 108, it correctly uses:
```typescript
if (this.operator === 'in' && this.right.variable instanceof NamespaceVariable)
```

But in line 123, it incorrectly uses:
```typescript
if (this.operator !== 'in' || !this.right.variable?.isNamespace) return UnknownValue;
```

The issue is that `isNamespace` is a property that's set on `NamespaceVariable` instances, but the check in line 123 is using optional chaining (`?.isNamespace`) which might not work correctly for all variable types.

        resolveId(id) {

        load(id) {
          if (id === '"'"'main.js'"'"') return inputMain;
          if (id === '"'"'unitless.js'"'"') return inputUnitless;
        }
      }]
    });

      console.log('"'"'✅ PASS: "in" check is preserved'"'"');
    } else {
      console.log('"'"'❌ FAIL: "in" check was optimized away'"'"');
    }

    console.error('"'"'Error:'"'"', error);
  }
}

let unitlessKeys = {
  };

function addUnitIfNeeded(name, value) {
  if (value == null || typeof value === 'boolean' || value === '') {
    return '';
  }

  if (typeof value === 'number' && value !== 0 && !(name in unitlessKeys) && !name.startsWith('--')) {
    return `${value}px`;
  }

  return String(value).trim();
}

export { addUnitIfNeeded as default };

+// Deep investigation to understand when the optimization triggers
+const rollup = require('./dist/rollup');
+
+// Test case 1: Simple object with direct property access
+const test1 = `
+let unitless = { flex: 1 };
+function test(name) { return name in unitless; }
+export default test;
+`;
+
+// Test case 2: Object imported as default
+const test2 = `
+import unitless from './simple-unitless';
+function test(name) { return name in unitless; }
+export default test;
+`;
+
+const simpleUnitless = `
+export default { flex: 1, fontWeight: 1 };
+`;
+
+// Test case 3: Namespace import (star import)
+const test3 = `
+import * as unitless from './simple-unitless';
+function test(name) { return name in unitless; }
+export default test;
+`;
+
+async function runTest(testName, inputCode, additionalFiles = {}) {
+  console.log(`\n${'='.repeat(60)}`);
+  console.log(`TEST: ${testName}`);
+  console.log('='.repeat(60));
+  
+  try {
+    const bundle = await rollup.rollup({
+      input: 'main.js',
+      plugins: [{
+        name: 'virtual',
+        resolveId(id) {
+          if (id === 'main.js') return id;
+          if (id in additionalFiles) return id;
+        },
+        load(id) {
+          if (id === 'main.js') return inputCode;
+          if (id in additionalFiles) return additionalFiles[id];
+        }
+      }]
+    });
+
+    const { output } = await bundle.generate({ format: 'es' });
+    
+    console.log('Generated code:');
+    console.log('-'.repeat(40));
+    console.log(output[0].code);
+    
+    // Analysis
+    const code = output[0].code;
+    const hasUnitlessKeys = code.includes('flex') || code.includes('fontWeight');
+    const hasInCheck = code.includes(' in ') && code.includes('unitless');
+    
+    console.log('\nAnalysis:');
+    console.log(`- Object properties preserved: ${hasUnitlessKeys ? '✅' : '❌'}`);
+    console.log(`- "in" check preserved: ${hasInCheck ? '✅' : '❌'}`);
+    
+  } catch (error) {
+    console.error('Error:', error);
+  }
+}
+
+async function runAllTests() {
+  await runTest('Direct object', test1);
+  await runTest('Default import', test2, { './simple-unitless': simpleUnitless });
+  await runTest('Namespace import', test3, { './simple-unitless': simpleUnitless });
+}
+
+runAllTests();
\ No newline at end of file

+import * as unitless from './unitless';
+
+function addUnitIfNeeded(name, value) {
+  if (value == null || typeof value === 'boolean' || value === '') {
+    return '';
+  }
+
+  if (typeof value === 'number' && value !== 0 && !(name in unitless) && !name.startsWith('--')) {
+    return \`\${value}px\`;
+  }
+
+  return String(value).trim();
+}
+
+// Force usage to avoid tree-shaking
+const result = addUnitIfNeeded('flex', 1);
+console.log(result);
+
+export { addUnitIfNeeded };
+`;
+
+const unitlessCode = `
+const unitlessKeys = {
+  animationIterationCount: 1,
+  aspectRatio: 1,
+  borderImageOutset: 1,
+  borderImageSlice: 1,
+  borderImageWidth: 1,
+  boxFlex: 1,
+  boxFlexGroup: 1,
+  boxOrdinalGroup: 1,
+  columnCount: 1,
+  columns: 1,
+  flex: 1,
+  flexGrow: 1,
+  flexPositive: 1,
+  flexShrink: 1,
+  flexNegative: 1,
+  flexOrder: 1,
+  gridRow: 1,
+  gridRowEnd: 1,
+  gridRowSpan: 1,
+  gridRowStart: 1,
+  gridColumn: 1,
+  gridColumnEnd: 1,
+  gridColumnSpan: 1,
+  gridColumnStart: 1,
+  fontWeight: 1,
+  lineHeight: 1,
+  opacity: 1,
+  order: 1,
+  orphans: 1,
+  scale: 1,
+  tabSize: 1,
+  widows: 1,
+  zIndex: 1,
+  zoom: 1,
+  WebkitLineClamp: 1,
+};
+
+export default unitlessKeys;
+`;
+
+async function build() {
+  try {
+    const bundle = await rollup.rollup({
+      input: 'main.js',
+      plugins: [{
+        name: 'virtual',
+        resolveId(id) {
+          if (id === 'main.js') return id;
+          if (id === './unitless') return 'unitless.js';
+        },
+        load(id) {
+          if (id === 'main.js') return inputCode;
+          if (id === 'unitless.js') return unitlessCode;
+        }
+      }]
+    });
+
+    const { output } = await bundle.generate({ format: 'es' });
+    
+    console.log('Generated code:');
+    console.log('='.repeat(80));
+    console.log(output[0].code);
+    console.log('='.repeat(80));
+    
+    // Deep analysis
+    const code = output[0].code;
+    
+    console.log('\nAnalysis:');
+    console.log('- Has unitless object:', code.includes('unitlessKeys') ? '✅' : '❌');
+    console.log('- Has "flex" property:', code.includes('flex') ? '✅' : '❌');
+    console.log('- Has "in" check:', code.includes(' in ') && code.includes('unitless') ? '✅' : '❌');
+    
+    // Check if the object properties are preserved
+    const preservedProps = ['flex', 'fontWeight', 'zIndex'].filter(prop => code.includes(prop));
+    console.log('- Preserved properties:', preservedProps.length > 0 ? preservedProps.join(', ') : '❌ None');
+    
+  } catch (error) {
+    console.error('Error:', error);
+  }
+}
+
+build();

+  columnCount: 1,
+  columns: 1,
+  flex: 1,
+  flexGrow: 1,
+  flexPositive: 1,
+  flexShrink: 1,
+  flexNegative: 1,
+  flexOrder: 1,
+  gridRow: 1,
+  gridRowEnd: 1,
+  gridRowSpan: 1,
+  gridRowStart: 1,
+  gridColumn: 1,
+  gridColumnEnd: 1,
+  gridColumnSpan: 1,

+  fontWeight: 1,

+  opacity: 1,
+  order: 1,
+  orphans: 1,
+  scale: 1,
+  tabSize: 1,
+  widows: 1,
+  zIndex: 1,
+  zoom: 1,
+  WebkitLineClamp: 1,
+};
+
+export default function addUnitIfNeeded(name, value) {
+  if (value == null || typeof value === 'boolean' || value === '') {
+    return '';
+  }
+
+  if (typeof value === 'number' && value !== 0 && !(name in unitlessKeys) && !name.startsWith('--')) {
+    return \`\${value}px\`; // Presumes implicit 'px' suffix for unitless numbers except for CSS variables
+  }
+
+  return String(value).trim();
+}
+`;
+

+          if (id === 'main.js') return id;
+        },

+          if (id === 'main.js') return inputCode;
+        }
+      }]
+    });
+
+    const { output } = await bundle.generate({ format: 'es' });
+    
+    console.log('Generated code:');
+    console.log('='.repeat(80));
+    console.log(output[0].code);
+    console.log('='.repeat(80));
+

+      console.log('❌ FAIL: unitlessKeys object was optimized away');
+      console.log('This breaks styled-components!');
+    }
+    
+    // Check if the "in" check is preserved

+      console.log('❌ FAIL: "in" check was optimized away');
+      console.log('This breaks styled-components!');
+    }

+build();

+// Test if tree-shaking is causing the issue
+const rollup = require('./dist/rollup');
+
+// Test case where the "in" check might be optimized away because the property is known
+const inputCode = `
+import * as unitless from './unitless';
+
+function test1() {
+  return 'flex' in unitless; // This should be statically knowable
+}
+
+function test2(name) {
+  return name in unitless; // This should not be optimized away
+}
+
+export { test1, test2 };
+`;
+
+const unitlessCode = `
+const unitlessKeys = {
+  flex: 1,
+  fontWeight: 1,
+  zIndex: 1
+};
+
+export default unitlessKeys;
+`;
+
+async function build() {
+  try {
+    const bundle = await rollup.rollup({
+      input: 'main.js',
+      plugins: [{
+        name: 'virtual',
+        resolveId(id) {
+          if (id === 'main.js') return id;
+          if (id === './unitless') return 'unitless.js';
+        },
+        load(id) {
+          if (id === 'main.js') return inputCode;
+          if (id === 'unitless.js') return unitlessCode;
+        }
+      }]
+    });
+
+    const { output } = await bundle.generate({ 
+      format: 'es',
+      generatedCode: 'es2015'
+    });
+    
+    console.log('Generated code:');
+    console.log('='.repeat(80));
+    console.log(output[0].code);
+    console.log('='.repeat(80));
+    
+    // Check for specific optimizations
+    const code = output[0].code;
+    
+    console.log('\nAnalysis:');
+    console.log('- Has unitlessKeys object:', code.includes('unitlessKeys') ? '✅' : '❌');
+    console.log('- Has "flex" in unitlessKeys:', code.includes('flex') ? '✅' : '❌');
+    console.log('- test1 optimized (no "in" check):', !code.includes(\`'flex' in unitless\`) ? '✅' : '❌');
+    console.log('- test2 has "in" check:', code.includes('name in unitless') ? '✅' : '❌');
+    
+  } catch (error) {
+    console.error('Error:', error);
+  }
+}
+
+build();
